<date>1612889882920<//date><Rate>5<//Rate><text>I ordered from here via DoorDash during COVID times so I can't speak on the physical restaurant.

We were visiting the Santa Cruz area last week and my partner and I were craving Indian food.  He spent all of last year there, while I went on vacation for a few weeks in India.  I have to say that I have no complaints about the food.  I'm not sure if we ordered on a good day, but everything was absolutely delicious.

We started off with the saag paneer.  This was probably my favorite dish of the bunch.  I'm a huge fan of paneer so I will definitely be ordering this again.  It was super flavorful and paired beautifully with some garlic naan.

We also ordered the mixed tandoori.  While in India, we had proper tandoori chicken.  Although, it tasted similar, it didn't quite hit the mark for me.  Don't get me wrong, it was still good, but I've had better.

Lastly, we had the chicken biriyani.  The chicken in this was soooooo tasty.  The chicken was so tender and beautifully seasoned.

I wasn't having high hopes for Indian food in Santa Cruz, but I can confidently say that this place is pretty good.  I would recommend trying it out if you are in the area.< /text>< pics>

I will admit that I am a biased customer of T-Mobile in CA and previously in Europe, but for a cell company I still feel that their customer service and offerings far surpass that of their rivals.  Their staff are ultimately focused on customer  service and yes, I may have had a few issues, but this store has always been abile to sort out any problems I may have had.

The store is easily accessible, clean and modern.  They have a good stock range, they are happy to let you browse and they do not act like second hand car salesmen and pressure you.  As for TMOBILE in general, I have found that their coverage is good, the prices beat their main stream competitiors and despite the appalling website, well worth considering, even if you are mid contact with someone else. But that's your fault for not using TMobile in the first place.<//text>

< Review>
This Tacos Mexico in particular is the best one. Been coming here since 1993, and like it as much now as I did the first time I decided to give it a shot. The food is delicious, the staff is very clean, and super friendly. My personal favorite is the BUCHE burrito Ortega the CARNITAS taco. Both with the red sauce. Make sure to request the salsa on the side, since it's a bit spicy. The music that auto plays from the juke box is a bit loud, but goes well with the atmosphere as well as the soccer channel on both TV's. It's a very small restaurant with indoor/outdoor seating. You should definitely stop by to try, I'm sure you'll like it as much as I do. And the prices are on the cheaper side too!< /Review>

< Text>
I've been to many other Tacos Mexico, and I would not recommend at all. This one, located in the tiny city of Bell is fantastic. The customer service is beyond good, these guys are always in the best of moods. Their good spirit reflects on the food... This little taco joint prepares and serves the best tacos, burritos, sopes, tostadas, and tortas infantiles the area. Trust me I know tacos, I grew up on them! And the prices are definitely cheap. For instance 1 burrito 2 tacos + soda will run you around $12, I truly recommend this place. Nothing fancy, just delicious food, great mood, and fantastic prices. Try the buche and or carnitas tacos with the red sauce! Oh, they also offer all you can eat grilled onions.
Thank you< /Text>
